\usepackage{tikz,forest}
\usetikzlibrary{arrows.meta}
\forestset{
default preamble={
before typesetting nodes={
  !r.replace by={[, coordinate, append]}
},  
where n children=0{
  tier=word,
}{  
  %diamond, aspect=2,
},  
where level=0{}{
  if n=1{
    edge label={node[pos=.2, above] {Y}},
  }{  
    edge label={node[pos=.2, above] {N}},
  }   
},  
for tree={
  edge+={thick, -Latex},
  s sep'+=2cm,
  draw,
  thick,
  edge path'={ (!u) -| (.parent)},
  align=center,
}   
}
